Each stretch of road is maintained by a separate Ranger, and you notice that each takes on the character of its overseer: some are pristine and run with military efficiency, while others have a characteristically Californian funk. Rick\'s seems to be one of the latter, including a display of trophies from foolish motorists who thought they could defy him. You feel fortunate to have him as an ally.
